> **✅ v4.73 CREATIVE ASSET SELECTION v0 BRIEF ACCEPTED (docs-only; PK-approved design brief; no build; 2026-07-02):** PK accepted the reframed **Creative Asset Selection v0 — Template Slot Matching & Safe Asset Choice** design brief (`docs/briefs/creative-asset-selection-v0-brief.md`). **Governing distinction:** **Asset Selection is SEPARATE from Asset Intake (v4.63)** — intake = how assets *enter*/become governed (NOT re-opened here); selection = how ICE *chooses* the right governed asset for a template slot at render time. **Asset Selection ASSUMES a template has already been chosen by upstream TMR / template-selection logic** (template selection is a separate future sibling brief, out of scope). **Scope = slot matching + safe asset choice ONLY.** **Production rule: no governed eligible asset → STOP (no production render).** **Smoke rule: neutral synthetic placeholder allowed ONLY for smoke/testing** (explicitly not a brand-ready asset). **Output-as-input is explicitly FORBIDDEN** (never feed a rendered/published output back as a source). **Fail-closed triggers:** unknown license · expired license · wrong client · missing release/consent · unsuitable platform · unsafe asset. Deliverables the design must produce: slot→asset-type→eligibility matrix, the 8-step filter/rank decision order, the fail-closed policy, and a thin Slice-1 (`Background.source` + `Logo.source` + possibly `Scrim.opacity` for the live dark static cards, read-only, off the production path). **NON-CLAIMS:** no schema · no DB mutation · no render · no proof event · no publish · no enablement · no binding · no platform_safe · no production_proven · no Format Mix claim. **NEXT (read-only, no build):** design pass *Creative Asset Selection v0 — Current-State Map + Slot Decision Model* (inspect real template `dynamic` fields, `resolve_brand_assets`, `client_brand_profile.brand_logo_url`, PP logo/background paths → produce the matrix + decision order + fail-closed policy + Slice-1); stop after the read-only design output. Supersedes → v4.72 (TMR static library complete + registry synced).

> **✅ v4.32 TMR-1 TEMPLATE METADATA REGISTRY v1 DESIGN — DEFINES THE CANONICAL METADATA MODEL ICE WILL USE TO ONBOARD / AUDIT / CLASSIFY / GOVERN PROVIDER TEMPLATES (Creatomate today, HeyGen/future later) AS A FIRST-CLASS REGISTRY SEPARATE FROM VARIANT BINDING (docs/design + register ONLY, 2026-06-30):** A design brief for the Template Metadata Registry — the TMR-1 slice. **This CE register pass = docs/design/registers ONLY — 0 Supabase table / 0 migration / 0 `execute_sql` / 0 CE function / 0 runtime-code change / 0 edge-function change / 0 dashboard-repo edit / 0 Content-Studio code / 0 CCF file edit / 0 `property-pulse.json` / 0 `creative_contract.ts` / 0 `registry-schema-v2.md` / 0 schema / 0 DB / 0 deploy / 0 provider-API call / 0 render / 0 publish / 0 template binding / 0 production enablement / 0 variant enablement / 0 secret-in-docs / 0 GFCP-Layer-3 / 0 canonical-model.** CE `main == origin/main == 502b31c8e39d915b1238239036bf2aa491d0b90b` (pre-edit; strict HEAD check passed). CCF-01 Phase 1 guards remain **dry-run / log-only**, **not modified** (no hook output appeared). **(1) Brief:** `docs/briefs/template-metadata-registry-v1-design.md` (new). **(2) Core principle (do NOT collapse):** **template family** (reusable pattern) ≠ **provider template** (exact external asset, an inventory object first) ≠ **field inventory** ≠ **output contract** ≠ **platform suitability** (first-class, per-platform) ≠ **format variant** (governed usage) ≠ **client/brand assignment** (scoped permission) ≠ **platform proof** (separate from capability). **(3) Problem:** ICE has creative-library/variant/proof records but **no DB-backed provider-template metadata table**; Creatomate is template-based; provider names may mislead (e.g. `news_quote_insight_1x1_v1` reads like a quote card but its elements are a market-insight/headline card); a template may be generic/brand/client/platform-specific or unassigned; ICE must know a template's fields before binding, which platforms it physically suits, and have full auditability. **(4) Model sections:** template family (key/name/purpose/default format+variant candidate/scope/vertical/status/timestamps; holds multiple provider templates across aspect ratios + platform/client/version); provider template (provider/id/name/family_key/scope/client_id?/brand_key?/width/height/aspect/output_type/file_type/duration?/sanitized project ref/inventory_status/source/captured_by+at/inventory_hash/status — **no secrets/keys/billing**); field inventory (element_id/name/type/track/dynamic/field_kind/default_value_safe?/style/constraints?/required_for_render?); output contract (dimensions/aspect/orientation/static-animated-video/duration/file type/safe formats/readability/text capacity — determines platform suitability); **platform suitability first-class per-platform** (platform/placement?/suitability_status unknown→candidate→not_suitable→needs_review→platform_safe→production_proven→blocked/reason/constraints/proof_reference?/last_reviewed_at; **suitability ≠ production proof**); variant candidate mapping (format_key/variant_key/fit_status incl. `strong_candidate`/`needs_template_edit`/`unsuitable`/fit_reason/required_field_mapping_status/missing_fields/reviewer); **client/brand assignment SEPARATE** (template_id/client_id?/brand_key?/assignment_scope/assignment_status/style_guide_reference/approver — where PP logo/colours/style/governance apply); governance+proof lifecycle `discovered → inventory_requested → inventory_captured → inventory_verified → classified → field_mapped → governance_reviewed → smoke_rendered → visually_approved → platform_safe → client_enabled → production_proven` (+deprecated/blocked) with **inventory_captured ≠ renderable ≠ platform_safe ≠ client_enabled ≠ production_proven**; audit (captured_by/at/capture_method/source_reference/inventory_hash/changed_fields/reviewer/decision/decision_reason/no_secret_assertion/no_mutation_assertion — **never store raw secrets**). **(5) Future Supabase (DESIGN ONLY, no tables):** candidate tables `creative_template_family` / `creative_provider_template` / `creative_provider_template_field` / `creative_template_platform_suitability` / `creative_template_variant_candidate` / `creative_template_client_assignment` / `creative_template_inventory_audit` / `creative_template_proof_event` — **DB creation = later TMR-2/TMR-3** (not this slice; no `registry-schema-v2.md` change). **(6) Relationships:** GFCP (global platform×format), Client Overlay (client×platform×format + proof), FVI (variant lifecycle), Creative Intake (operator flow/wizard data model), Creative Library (proven registry), Format Mix (uses only after proof) — **KEY RULE: TMR *feeds* these systems; TMR does NOT itself enable production publishing.** **(7) Example classification (illustrative, non-binding) — `490ad9ea-7473-49e4-9d3c-e1ae8a12d790`:** creatomate / `news_quote_insight_1x1_v1` / 1080×1080 / 1:1 / static_image; fields Background + Scrim(fixed) + CategoryBadge + Logo + Headline + Subtitle + Location + Date + Footer; likely family `generic.real_estate.market_insight_card`; platform candidates fb/ig/linkedin feed image; variant candidates **market_update.v1 = strong/promising candidate**, **quote_card.v1 = needs_template_edit**, news_card.v1 = candidate-needs-review — **NOT a binding / NOT enablement / NOT render proof / example only.** **CARRIES (recorded):** **(C1)** TMR-2/TMR-3 (DB tables → migration → security review → apply under PK gate) — later, gated; **(C2)** the CI-4 family of unblock slices (CI-4C manual sanitized export, CI-4D endpoint design packet, CI-4E security review, CI-4F implement read-only inventory endpoint, CI-4G dashboard inventory display, CI-4H classify) — later, gated; **(C3)** quote_card.v1 = **needs_template_edit**, still BLOCKED at template_inventory_captured/binding; market_update.v1 = strong candidate but still DEFINED/unwired (needs definition → governance → render proof → platform proof); **(C4)** CI-3A/CI-3B; **(C5)** CI-5 HeyGen inventory model; **(C6)** CI-2 wizard slices CI-2A..CI-2F; **(C7)** CI-1 server-side read model; **(C8)** CI-6 explicit variant-intent request model; **(C9)** GFCP Layer 3 read-only projection (D-V3) — later; > **✅ v4.31 PROVIDER INVENTORY READ ACCESS PATTERN v1 — DEFINES THE APPROVED SAFE PATTERN FOR READING PROVIDER TEMPLATE/ASSET INVENTORY WITHOUT EXPOSING SECRETS OR MUTATING PROVIDER STATE (Creatomate first, then HeyGen/future; resolves how to remove the CI-4 BLOCKED_NO_SAFE_READ_PATH blocker durably; CI-4 blocker UNCHANGED — no safe read path exists today; docs/design/security + register ONLY, 2026-06-30):** A design/security brief for the provider inventory read access pattern — the CI-4B slice. **This CE register pass = docs/design/security/registers ONLY — 0 endpoint impl / 0 provider connector / 0 Creatomate-API call / 0 HeyGen-API call / 0 provider mutation / 0 render / 0 publish / 0 dashboard-repo edit / 0 CE function / 0 runtime-code change / 0 edge-function change / 0 Content-Studio code / 0 `property-pulse.json` / 0 `creative_contract.ts` / 0 `registry-schema-v2.md` / 0 schema / 0 DB / 0 `execute_sql` / 0 migration / 0 deploy / 0 production enablement / 0 variant enablement / 0 secret printed-or-stored / 0 GFCP-Layer-3 / 0 canonical-model.** CE `main == origin/main == e9b3d070a78f1fa9f1e261d92da0f751b204e701` (pre-edit; strict HEAD re-check passed — CI-4 shared-worktree race noted, no drift this slice). **(1) Brief:** `docs/briefs/provider-inventory-read-access-pattern-v1.md` (new) + a one-line cross-reference added to `docs/briefs/format-variant-quote-card-creatomate-template-inventory.md` (CI-4 next-action → CI-4B). **(2) CI-4 blocker UNCHANGED:** **no safe read path currently exists.** **(3) Problem:** Creative Intake needs provider inventory but secrets must not be exposed and reads must not mutate provider state; concrete blocker = `quote_card.v1` needs Creatomate inventory for `490ad9ea-7473-49e4-9d3c-e1ae8a12d790`; the CE worker path can't safely read (`CREATOMATE_API_KEY` is a `Deno.env` runtime secret; workers call only `/v2/renders`; no metadata-read endpoint); a local/manual call would expose the secret (forbidden); the render path creates a render (not pure inventory). **(4) Security principles:** secrets stay server-side only; never print/store API keys; never paste raw secret-bearing payloads in docs; separate read-only metadata endpoints from render/mutation; sanitize responses; least privilege; audit reads; inventory read ≠ enablement; inventory read ≠ render proof; inventory read does not auto-update Creative Library truth without review. **(5) Options:** **A — server-side read-only Edge Function** (holds secret server-side; accepts provider/object_type/object_id; metadata read only; returns sanitized summary; no render/mutate/upload/edit/publish; audit without secret; controls = allowlisted provider+object types, allowlisted endpoint paths, no arbitrary URL fetch, no raw passthrough unless redacted, response sanitizer, timeout/retry limits, audit log, service-role/server-only, no browser-direct secret path, deny mutation verbs/endpoints; tests = sanitizer/deny-list/allowlist/no-secret-log/no-mutation/contract; **RECOMMENDED durable path**). **B — connector/MCP read-only provider tool** (secret outside CE; sanitized inventory; acceptable IF available + read-only scope enforceable; **none exists today**). **C — PK manual sanitized export** (PK exports/pastes sanitized element inventory; zero CE secret handling; acceptable **SHORT-TERM one-off unblock**; checklist required). **D — render-probe** (**NOT acceptable** as inventory read; costs money + mutates render state; only as a separately-authorized smoke/render proof, never default). **(6) Recommended path:** short-term **Option C** one-off unblock for `quote_card` if PK can safely export/paste; durable product path **Option A** server-side read-only inventory endpoint; **Option B** connector acceptable if available + read-only; **DO NOT** use Option D as default. **(7) Creatomate read pattern (future):** return sanitized template id/name/dimensions/aspect/duration + elements (id-name/type/dynamic flag/accepted value type/default-present flag without leaking content)/output type/constraints; **MUST NOT** return API keys/account secrets/billing/unrelated project data/raw assets if unnecessary/arbitrary workspace listing unless authorized. **(8) HeyGen/future:** same pattern; HeyGen identity/persona/voice/scene oriented; reads must not create avatars/videos; consent/persona governance metadata treated carefully; future providers implement an inventory adapter with safe normalized output. **(9) Audit model (design only, no DB table):** provider/object_type/object_id/requested_by/requested_at/read_method/sanitizer_version/returned_inventory_hash/status/error_class/no_secret_assertion/no_mutation_assertion. **(10) quote_card application:** `quote_card.v1` **remains blocked**; next unblock = (A) PK manual sanitized export of `490ad9ea`, or (B) safe read-only inventory endpoint/connector; **NO binding** until inventory captured AND field mapping reviewed. **(11) Future slices (NOT implemented):** CI-4C PK manual sanitized export checklist for `490ad9ea`; CI-4D server-side read-only inventory endpoint design packet; CI-4E security review; CI-4F implement Creatomate read-only inventory endpoint; CI-4G dashboard read-only inventory display; CI-4H classify quote_card readiness from captured inventory. **CARRIES (recorded):** **(C1)** CI-4C..CI-4H slices above — later, gated; **(C2)** quote_card.v1 still **BLOCKED** at `template_inventory_captured` (no safe read path today); **(C3)** CI-3A/CI-3B; **(C4)** CI-5 HeyGen inventory model; **(C5)** CI-2 wizard slices CI-2A..CI-2F; > **✅ v4.29 CI-3 PROVIDER INVENTORY CAPTURE MODEL v1 — DEFINES WHAT 'PROVIDER INVENTORY CAPTURE' MEANS ACROSS CREATOMATE / HEYGEN / FUTURE PROVIDERS (the info the Creative Intake wizard must collect about a provider template/asset BEFORE a template/variant can move beyond defined; inventory capture is READ-ONLY fact-gathering, NOT enablement; docs/design + register ONLY, 2026-06-30):** A design brief for the provider inventory capture model — the CI-3 slice of the CE v4.26 Creative Intake Operator Flow. **This CE register pass = docs/design/registers ONLY — 0 connector / 0 provider-API (Creatomate/HeyGen) call / 0 dashboard-repo edit / 0 CE function / 0 runtime-code change / 0 Content-Studio code / 0 `property-pulse.json` / 0 `creative_contract.ts` / 0 `registry-schema-v2.md` / 0 schema / 0 DB / 0 `execute_sql` / 0 migration / 0 deploy / 0 render / 0 publish / 0 production enablement / 0 variant enablement / 0 GFCP-Layer-3 / 0 canonical-model.** CE `main == origin/main == 65550c0aef50c61812d00c63ff34ca306b0d3918` (pre-edit). **(1) Brief:** `docs/briefs/creative-intake-provider-inventory-capture-model-v1.md` (new). **(2) Where it sits:** CI-1 shows status (shipped v4.27); CI-2 wizard creates intake drafts (spec v4.28); CI-3 (this) = what to collect per provider before binding; CI-4/CI-5 connectors later. **(3) Foundational rule:** inventory capture is **read-only fact-gathering, NOT enablement** — capturing inventory does NOT govern/render/prove/enable anything; `captured` ≠ `governed` ≠ `renderable` ≠ `production_proven`; AI/operator proposes, gates + PK approve. **(4) Purpose:** records what a provider template/asset can **accept and produce** (object exists / inputs / outputs / dynamic vs fixed / proof available / still missing); prerequisite for the `template_inventory_captured` + `field_mapped` gates. **(5) Standard (provider-neutral) model:** core identity (provider / object type / object id / object name / source / captured_at / captured_by / inventory_status); format-output (output_format / aspect / dimensions / duration / render_kind static-animated-video-avatar-voice / supported platforms); input contract (required + optional fields / types / max lengths / media types / language-voice-avatar fields / background+asset slots / logo+brand slots); output contract (asset type / file type / resolution / duration / audio / captions / safe zones / platform constraints); evidence (source / screenshot / sanitized metadata / render proof / visual approval / known limitations); provider-specific detail stays in the **adapter**, common ICE layer stores only a **normalized summary + safe metadata**. **(6) Statuses:** `missing` / `requested` / `captured_from_docs` / `captured_from_provider_read` / `captured_from_manual_entry` / `captured_from_render_probe` / `verified` / `stale` / `blocked` — `captured` ≠ `governed`; `verified` ≠ `renderable`; render proof is a separate gate; inventory ≠ production proof. **(7) Creatomate model (composition-based):** identity (template id / name / workspace-if-safe / mode image-template|video-source|composition); structure (element list names+types, dynamic vs fixed, text/image/video/audio/shape-scrim-background/logo-brand fields); output (dimensions/aspect/duration/file type/static-vs-animated); field mapping (ICE field → Creatomate element, required/optional, max length, fallback, missing-element handling); **SAFETY** (no provider mutation during read, no API-key exposure in docs, store only safe metadata, no raw secrets, no render unless separately authorized). Reference: proven sibling `fb9820f8` exposes 6 text + 2 image slots (illustrative); quote_card candidate `news_quote_insight_1x1_v1` template `490ad9ea-7473-49e4-9d3c-e1ae8a12d790` = status **blocked / inventory MISSING** (Slice 3D pending safe read) — inventory required before binding. **(8) HeyGen model (identity/persona-based):** identity (object type avatar/talking_photo/voice/scene-background/template, object id, display name if safe, ownership/brand scope); inputs (narration_text/script, voice id, avatar/talking_photo id, background/scene, language/accent, duration, aspect, captions); governance (avatar/persona approval, voice approval, scene approval, brand fit, policy, consent/ownership); output (video format/resolution/duration/audio/language/platform constraints) — **HeyGen is identity/persona-driven** (talking_photo + voice + TTS + single scene; avatars provisioned on a separate asset path), **NOT** Creatomate-style element-driven; captures identities + governance, not an element list. **(9) Future provider:** adapter declares object type / input contract / output contract / capability limits / proof-evidence type / inventory-capture source; provider-specific fields stay in adapter; common layer stores normalized summary + safe metadata. **(10) Wizard relationship:** wizard may request inventory; cannot mark `field_mapped` without inventory; cannot mark `renderable` without render proof; cannot mark `executable` from inventory alone; missing inventory ⇒ `blocked_needs_provider_inventory`. **(11) Proof gates:** FVI `defined` can exist before inventory; `template_inventory_captured` needs inventory; `field_mapped` needs ICE→provider mapping; `governed` needs PK/style/policy; `renderable` needs successful render; `production_proven` needs publish evidence. **(12) Security:** never store API keys; never paste secrets in docs; reads read-only; sanitize metadata; redact raw payloads; record only safe ids/names/field metadata; no provider mutation; no auto-enablement after capture; unsafe-credential read = **hard stop** (Slice 3D precedent). **(13) Examples (no overclaim):** `news_card.v1` inventory/proof effectively satisfied via proven binding + renders; `quote_card.v1` **BLOCKED** (`490ad9ea` inventory missing); `market_update.v1` defined but no provider template/inventory yet; HeyGen/avatar future (capture avatar/voice/scene/script/persona governance before render). **(14) Future slices (NOT implemented):** CI-3A static inventory schema refinement; CI-3B dashboard read-only inventory detail card; CI-4 Creatomate read-only inventory connector (Slice 3D unblock); CI-5 HeyGen inventory model; CI-2A/B wizard prototype references inventory requirements; later server-backed inventory records. **CARRIES (recorded):** **(C1)** CI-3A/CI-3B + the CI-4/CI-5 connectors — later, gated; **(C2)** quote_card.v1 template inventory still **BLOCKED** pending safe Creatomate read; **(C3)** CI-2 wizard implementation slices (CI-2A..CI-2F) — later; **(C4)** CI-1 server-side read model — later; **(C5)** CI-6 explicit variant-intent request model; **(C6)** market_update.v1 / quote_card.v1 remain DEFINED / unwired (no proof borrowed; news_card.v1 default + proven PP × fb+ig only); **(C7)** GFCP Layer 3 read-only projection (D-V3) — later; **(C8)** FVI dashboard/overlay surfacing — later; **(C9)** DB-backed variant store / Canonical Capability Model v1 — future, not started; **(C10)** pre-existing template-family `property-pulse-news` `approved_at:null` (advisory); **(C11)** dashboard `lib/creative-library/registry.ts` v0.2 re-vendor carry. **EXPLICIT NON-CLAIMS / SCOPE (no overclaim):** this is a **design brief ONLY** — **no connector/provider call, no dashboard/runtime/Content-Studio code change, no `property-pulse.json`/`creative_contract.ts`/`registry-schema-v2.md`/schema/DB/migration change, no render/publish, no Creatomate/HeyGen API call, no production enablement, no format or variant enabled**; CI-2 (this spec) would **create** new intake requests; CI-3..CI-6 later. **(3) Foundational rule:** the wizard **creates + proves, never enables-by-creating** — its output is a `proposed`/`defined` intake request, **NOT executable, NOT enabled, NOT production-capable**; `defined` ≠ executable; AI/operator proposes, gates + PK approve. **(4) Entry (design only, no button in CI-2):** the Creative Intake page `/create/creative-intake` → a "New Template" / "Start intake" action. **(5) Wizard steps (capture-only; no render/provider/mutation/enable):** (1) client/brand + scope (global/client-specific/pilot-only); (2) platform(s) + format (existing `ice_format_key`) + output type (static image/animated image/carousel/short video/avatar video/voice video/long video) + aspect + platform constraints; (3) provider (Creatomate/HeyGen/future) + mode (composition-template/avatar-identity/voice-narration/generated-image/custom-adapter); (4) variant identity (proposed `variant_key`/name/family/version/purpose + kind new/replacement/manual-only/future-automated-candidate — candidate flags **intent only**, NOT automated selection); (5) content field contract (Creatomate: headline/subtitle/quote_text/stat/callout/location/date/source_context/background_image/logo; HeyGen: narration_text/script/avatar_role/talking_photo/voice id/scene/language/duration); (8) governance checklist (style guide/assets/logo/tone/policy/citation/avatar+voice approval/human approver) — PK-owned, not self-approved; (9) proof plan = the v4.26 gates `proposed → defined → template_inventory_captured → field_mapped → governed → smoke_tested → renderable → visually_approved → platform_safe → client_enabled → production_proven`; (10) review + submit → `intake_request_id`(future)/`variant_key`/provider/format/field contract/missing gates/next action, **initial state = `proposed` or `defined` ONLY, NOT executable, NOT enabled**. **(6) Output states:** `draft_intake`/`proposed`/`defined`/`blocked_needs_provider_inventory`/`blocked_needs_governance`/`blocked_needs_render_proof`/`blocked_needs_platform_safety`; **MUST NOT output `production_proven`/`executable`/`automated_enabled`** unless later gates prove it. **(7) Guardrails (shown in-wizard):** creating a template does not enable it; `defined` ≠ executable; provider-template-existing ≠ proven; smoke test ≠ production proof; unapproved variants cannot be offered in Studio; **automated selection requires a separate selector decision (v4.24)**. **(8) Provider differences:** one wizard, adapter-shaped Step 7 (Creatomate composition/template vs HeyGen avatar/identity vs future adapter declaring input/output contract + proof evidence + safety); common layer = `provider/format/variant/input contract/output contract/proof state/evidence/eligibility`. **(9) PP examples (no overclaim):** A `news_card.v1` already production-proven (PP × fb+ig only) — wizard would NOT create it now, shows a *completed* intake; > **✅ v4.26 CREATIVE INTAKE OPERATOR FLOW v1 — DESIGN BRIEF FOR THE FUTURE OPERATOR PATH FROM TEMPLATE IDEA TO GOVERNED/PROVEN CAPABILITY ACROSS PROVIDERS (defines an operator-friendly dashboard intake flow for CREATING and PROVING new creative templates/variants across Creatomate, HeyGen, and future providers — without letting an unproven template/variant become executable; standardises the intake STAGES + PROOF GATES while keeping provider inventory models adapter-specific; docs/design + register ONLY, 2026-06-30):** A design brief for the future dashboard/operator flow to **create and prove** new creative templates and variants across providers (Creatomate, HeyGen, future), in plain operator terms ("I want to make a new creative template") guided through format → sizes → provider → fields → governance → smoke → compliance → capability proof → approval → production proof. **This CE register pass = docs/design/registers ONLY — 0 UI build / 0 dashboard-repo edit / 0 Content-Studio code / 0 CE function / 0 runtime-code change / 0 `property-pulse.json` edit / 0 `creative_contract.ts` change / 0 `registry-schema-v2.md` edit / 0 schema / 0 DB / 0 `execute_sql` / 0 migration / 0 deploy / 0 render / 0 publish / 0 Creatomate-API call / 0 HeyGen-API call / 0 provider API call / 0 production enablement / 0 GFCP-Layer-3 / 0 template binding / 0 quote_card-or-market_update render proof / 0 format-or-variant enablement.** CE `main == origin/main == 44544f4e2f8a48c263ab0b274f5bcdc68c6075a1` (pre-edit). **(1) Brief:** `docs/briefs/creative-intake-operator-flow-v1.md` (new). **(2) Where it sits:** Creative Intake is the **production front-of-house** that **creates + proves** a variant/template **before** FVI eligibility / GFCP / Client Overlay / Content Studio can offer or execute it (dependency order: **Creative Intake → FVI → GFCP & Client Overlay → Content Studio**). **(3) Foundational rule:** intake **creates + proves, never enables-by-creating**; `defined` ≠ executable; provider-template-exists ≠ governed/renderable; rendered-once ≠ platform_safe; `production_proven` needs real **publish** evidence; AI/operator proposes, gates + PK approve. **(4) Operator goal + actions:** create template / create variant / link provider template / request provider inventory / submit for governance / run smoke test / request visual approval / promote after proof. **(5) Intake stages:** (1) scope (client/platform/format/variant-or-new/manual-vs-automated/provider); (2) template requirements (output type static-image/animated/video/avatar-video/voice-video/carousel · size/aspect · duration · fields: text/image/background/logo/avatar/voice/animation/audio/captions); (6) **proof gates** `proposed → defined → template_inventory_captured → field_mapped → governed → smoke_tested → renderable → visually_approved → platform_safe → client_enabled → production_proven` (+deprecated/blocked) — smoke_tested ≠ production_proven, defined ≠ executable, provider-template-exists ≠ enough, rendered-once ≠ platform_safe, production_proven needs real publish; (7) dashboard status (complete/blocked/missing-proof/next-action, manual-only vs automated-eligible, Studio-visible?, Format-Mix-visible?). **(6) Standard vs provider-specific:** ICE standardises **stages + proof gates**; does NOT force one template schema; common layer = `provider / format / variant / input contract / output contract / proof state / evidence / eligibility`; provider specifics stay inside adapters (mirrors the RI abstraction submit/poll/cost/capabilities/renderMode). **(7) Failure rules (fail closed):** no provider inventory → cannot bind; no field mapping → cannot render; no governance → cannot approve; no smoke render → cannot mark renderable; no visual approval → cannot publish manually; no platform proof → cannot mark platform_safe; no client eligibility → cannot expose to client Studio; no production proof → cannot mark production_proven; no explicit selector decision → cannot automate. **(8) PP examples (no overclaim):** `news_card.v1` = production_proven **PP × facebook+instagram ONLY** (default+active); > **✅ v4.25 CONTENT STUDIO CAPABILITY GUIDANCE v1 — DESIGN/GUARDRAIL BRIEF FOR HOW A FUTURE CONTENT STUDIO CONSUMES ICE CAPABILITY TRUTH (defines the future Content Studio guardrails so manual content creation can request formats/variants WITHOUT bypassing capability proof, client eligibility, platform safety, or governance — gated by Global Format Capability + Client Capability Overlay + Format Variant Intake + the v4.24 selector decision; docs/design + register ONLY, 2026-06-30):** A design/guardrail brief for how a FUTURE Content Studio should **consume** ICE capability truth, so **manual** content creation can request formats and variants **without bypassing** capability proof, client eligibility, platform safety, or governance. **This CE register pass = docs/design/registers ONLY — 0 UI build / 0 Content-Studio code / 0 CE function / 0 runtime-code change / 0 dashboard-repo edit / 0 `property-pulse.json` edit / 0 `creative_contract.ts` change / 0 `registry-schema-v2.md` edit / 0 schema / 0 DB / 0 `execute_sql` / 0 migration / 0 deploy / 0 render / 0 publish / 0 Creatomate-API call / 0 production enablement / 0 GFCP-Layer-3 / 0 template binding / 0 quote_card-or-market_update render proof / 0 format-or-variant enablement.** CE `main == origin/main == dc450647cf8446207a810c14ae41089895a9a025` (pre-edit). **(1) Brief:** `docs/briefs/content-studio-capability-guidance-v1.md` (new). **(2) Foundational rule:** Content Studio is a **consumer** of capability truth, **never a source of it** — `defined` ≠ `executable`; AI/operator proposes, the gates + PK approve. **(3) What Studio may request:** `client` / `platform` / `format` (existing `ice_format_key`) / **optional `variant_key`** / `content_intent` / `source` payload / `manual_approval_state` — **but the request is NOT auto-executable.** **(4) Gate chain (in order):** (1) **GFCP** — is `platform × format` globally supported/proven vs blocked/conflicted; (2) **Client Overlay** — is this client allowed/safe (R-MAP1 global conflict outranks client block; R-MAP2 `globally_available_client_disabled` ≠ `needs_client_setup`); (3) **FVI** — if a `variant_key` is supplied it must be that **EXACT** variant **governed AND eligible**; (4) **selector-default** — no `variant_key` ⇒ safe **default only** (PP `image_quote` ⇒ `news_card.v1`); (5) **platform safety** on the rendered asset; (6) **human approval** before publish for manual Studio. **(5) Explicit variant-intent rule (from v4.24):** manual/Studio explicit variant intent is the **next safe selector evolution** (Option 5 → Option 2) and Studio is the **first** safe place for it (operator-driven + approval-gated); resolver may select the requested variant **only if eligible**; **default fallback stays `news_card.v1`**; `quote_card.v1` / `market_update.v1` must **NOT** be selected merely because `defined`; missing/ineligible ⇒ fail closed or documented-policy fallback. **(6) UI guidance (future):** show only safe/eligible formats by default; blocked/conflicted shown **disabled with reason**; defined-but-unwired variants shown **'not available yet' (not selectable)**; production-proven shown **distinctly** from defined/unproven; warn on global conflict; **never publish from an unproven/unapproved variant**; distinguish **format availability vs client enablement vs variant eligibility vs render proof vs publish proof**. **(7) Manual vs automated:** automated scheduling stays conservative (no content-class/variant-mix; Options 3/4 deferred); Studio offers **explicit** operator choice, not automated classification; any future automated selector separately proven. **(8) Minimal future path (NOT implemented):** read-only Studio capability read-model/status FIRST → optional `variant_key` → eligibility check → manual approval gate → render-proof gate → publish gate → dashboard surfacing. **(9) Failure policy:** unsupported global format → block; client disabled → block/setup-required; global conflict → review-required; variant defined-only → block from render; variant missing inventory/template → block; variant requested-but-ineligible → fail closed; fallback only under explicit documented policy (default = **fail closed**). **(10) PP examples (no overclaim):** PP fb `image_quote` no `variant_key` ⇒ `news_card.v1` (default); +`news_card.v1` ⇒ eligible (proven PP × fb); IG +`news_card.v1` ⇒ eligible (proven PP × ig); +`quote_card.v1` ⇒ **BLOCKED** (defined only, no template inventory — Slice 3D BLOCKED pending safe Creatomate read — no render proof); +`market_update.v1` ⇒ **BLOCKED** (defined only, no template binding/render proof). **(11) Recommendation:** Content Studio is the **first place** to support explicit variant intent, **gated by GFCP + Client Overlay + Variant Intake**; do NOT expose unproven variants as executable; **build read-only guidance/status before editable execution.** **CARRIES (recorded):** **(C1)** read-only Studio capability read-model / status surface = the next *buildable* step (separately authorized, gated); **(C2)** optional `variant_key` + eligibility-check + manual-approval + render-proof + publish gates = later, separately-gated runtime slices that must NOT change the conservative automated default; **(C3)** quote_card.v1 template inventory still BLOCKED pending safe Creatomate read (Slice 3D); **(C4)** quote_card.v1 / market_update.v1 forward path (template inventory → template-definition/registry variant → governed ratification → render proof → visual approval → platform safety → explicit variant-intent → only later automated selection); **(C5)** GFCP Layer 3 read-only projection (D-V3) — not started; **(C6)** FVI dashboard/overlay surfacing — later, gated; **(C7)** DB-backed variant store (D-V1 future) / Canonical Capability Model v1 — not started; **(C8)** pre-existing template-family `property-pulse-news` `approved_at:null` (advisory); **(C9)** dashboard `lib/creative-library/registry.ts` v0.2 re-vendor carry. **EXPLICIT NON-CLAIMS / SCOPE (no overclaim):** this is a **design/guardrail brief ONLY** — **no UI built, no runtime/Content-Studio/dashboard code change, no `property-pulse.json`/`creative_contract.ts`/schema/DB/migration change, no render/publish, no Creatomate call, no production enablement, no format or variant enabled**; `quote_card.v1` / `market_update.v1` remain **`defined` only / unwired** (NOT governed/renderable/platform_safe/client_enabled/production_proven); `news_card.v1` remains the **default + production-proven** variant (PP × facebook+instagram only), no proof borrowed. **DO NOT START (unprompted):** Studio capability read-model/status build · optional `variant_key` plumbing · eligibility/approval/render/publish gates · GFCP Layer 3 · template binding · quote_card/market_update render proof · dashboard surfacing — all gated. > **✅ v4.24 FORMAT VARIANT SELECTOR — PK DECISION RECORDED FOR MULTI-VARIANT PROPERTY PULSE image_quote (the automated path stays one active variant per client × format = news_card.v1; quote_card.v1 / market_update.v1 stay defined/unwired; manual/Content-Studio explicit variant-intent is the next safe evolution; content-class + variant-mix deferred; NO runtime/binding change; docs/design/registers only, 2026-06-30):** PK has recorded the **selector-model decision** for multi-variant Property Pulse `image_quote`, before any template binding or runtime work. **This CE register pass = docs/design/registers only — 0 binding / 0 CE function / 0 DB / 0 migration / 0 `execute_sql` / 0 deploy / 0 RPC/grant change / 0 runtime-code change / 0 `creative_contract.ts` change / 0 `property-pulse.json` edit / 0 schema edit / 0 render / 0 publish / 0 Creatomate-API call / 0 render-selection change / 0 publisher / 0 Advisor / 0 Content-Studio change / 0 production enablement / 0 GFCP-Layer-3 / 0 dashboard surfacing.** CE `main == origin/main == c7aa3b319e7d518409f9b83c5661f60578e48baf` (pre-edit). **(1) Decision record:** `docs/briefs/format-variant-selector-decision-record.md` (new). **(2) Decision:** **KEEP Option 1 NOW** — one active *automated* variant per client × format; for PP `image_quote` the automated/default variant **remains `property_pulse.image_quote.news_card.v1`**. **ADOPT Option 5 → Option 2 (next, gated):** manual / Content-Studio **explicit variant intent** first, then explicit-variant resolver support (a future manual/Studio request *may* carry a requested `variant_key`; the resolver *may* select it **only if governed + eligible**; **default fallback remains `news_card.v1`**). **DEFER Option 3** (content-class selector) and **Option 4** (weighted variant mix) until explicit-intent is proven. **No runtime change is authorized by this record.** **(3) Why a decision was needed:** the current gate is format-level only (`resolveCreativeContract(client_id, recommended_format='image_quote')` → single `news_card` contract; ai-worker stamps additively); `(client, format)` is **1:1**, so multiple variants per `(client, format)` are unrepresentable today (the Slice 3A NEEDS_SCHEMA_DECISION co-requisite). **(4) Safety rules (binding):** no implicit second variant under the same `(client, format)` gate; > **✅ v4.04 H3.2 RENDER RETRY CAP (pipeline-fixer) — SHIPPED + VERIFIED (failed-image retry loop now bounded; this register pass docs/registers only, 2026-06-26):** **H3.2** — `pipeline-fixer`'s `fixFailedImages` now **caps render retries** so a permanently-broken draft is dead-lettered instead of looping `failed → pending → render → failed` forever (the worst observed draft had accumulated **121 failed/timeout render rows**, burning Creatomate credits). **The H3.2 code + deploy landed earlier this lane (commit `abb89c47`); this register pass = docs/registers only — 0 app / 0 function / 0 DB / 0 migration / 0 deploy / 0 backfill / 0 dashboard UI.** CE `main == origin/main == abb89c47`; **pipeline-fixer v1.2.0 deployed as platform version 36, `verify_jwt=false` confirmed**. **Closes the v4.03 OPEN CARRY ("H3.2 retry cap remains OPEN").** **(1) Scope (single-render image formats ONLY):** caps **`image_quote`, `animated_text_reveal`, `animated_data`** (one render per draft → one failed row per attempt → row-count == attempt-count). **Carousel EXCLUDED in v1** (a carousel attempt renders ~5–6 slides → up to ~6 failed rows per *single* attempt, so a raw row-count cap would false-positive after one attempt; carousel is also bounded ≤12, not the runaway risk). **(2) Source of truth:** a **fresh count of `m.post_render_log` rows with `status IN ('failed','timeout')`** for the draft, computed at fix time — **NOT** the stored `attempt_number` (failure-scoped + authoritative, and sidesteps the accepted H3.1 telemetry race entirely by not consuming it). **(3) Cap N = 5** (matches the existing youtube-publisher `max_attempts:n/5` precedent + calibration {≥5: 11 drafts, ≥10: 9, worst: 121}; genuine transient failures still retry up to 4×). **(4) Terminal state:** at `failCount ≥ 5` the draft is **NOT reset** — `image_status` **stays `'failed'`** (valid CHECK value), **`dead_reason='render_attempts_exhausted'`** is set, `updated_at` bumped, and the candidate SELECT gains `dead_reason IS NULL` so it is **not re-evaluated**. **`approval_status` UNCHANGED** (stays `approved`, per directive — publishers already hard-block `image_status='failed'` via `asset_backstop`, so no new publish/queue exposure). **No DB migration** (`dead_reason` + `image_status` pre-exist; change is SELECT/UPDATE on `m.post_draft` columns the fixer already writes). **(5) Live verification (PK-run):** first cron run **2026-06-26 11:25:05 UTC succeeded** — `health_ok=true`, **`fixes_applied=[]` (clean no-op)**, `dead_reason='render_attempts_exhausted'` count = **0** (current approved+failed image backlog = 0 → the cap is **preventive**; deploy retroactively dead-letters **nothing**); pipeline-fixer logs **200 / no error spike**. *(Note: an observed `pipeline-ai-summary` 500 was **unrelated** and **not a regression** of this change.)* **(6) Gate trail (build lane):** brief / design packet (`docs/briefs/h3-2-retry-cap-design-packet.md`) → ef-builder (isolated worktree) → Deno tests (8 cases incl. below-cap reset / at-cap dead-letter / carousel-uncapped / already-exhausted-skipped / generated-untouched) → branch-warden `safe` → `ask_chatgpt_review` on the final diff → PK deploy gate (HARD STOP) → **PK-run deploy `--no-verify-jwt`** (`verify_jwt=false` confirmed). `db-rls-auditor` **not required** (no DDL / no migration / no new function / no grant/RLS change / no new REST surface). Code commit `abb89c47` touched **only** `supabase/functions/pipeline-fixer/index.ts` + `index.test.ts`. **FUTURE CARRIES (recorded, NOT started):** **H3.2b — carousel cap** (round-aware count `count(DISTINCT attempt_number) FILTER (status IN failed/timeout)`, now feasible because H3.1 populates `attempt_number` forward) · **H3.3 — dashboard visibility** of `render_attempts_exhausted` dead-letters (OPTIONAL operator-surfacing carry; `ai-diagnostic` already rolls up the reason — it is **not** in the `%housekeeping%`/`%backlog%`/`%auditor%` filter — so exhaustion already surfaces in diagnostics; a dedicated dashboard view is the optional next step). **DO NOT START (unprompted):** H3.2b carousel cap · H3.3 dashboard visibility · B1-v2 · broad Creative Library production wiring · further pipeline-fixer changes · dashboard work. Authority impact: **H3.2 now STOPS the failed-image retry loop after 5 failed/timeout renders for the three capped single-render formats** (terminal `failed` + `dead_reason`); carousel + all non-image formats + queue/publish paths + render content paths + governance + roadmap[`04_phases`] + T1 unchanged; AI proposes, PK approves. Supersedes → v4.03 (H3.1 attempt_number auto-compute).

> **✅ v4.03 H3.1 `write_render_log` ATTEMPT_NUMBER AUTO-COMPUTE — APPLIED + VERIFIED (telemetry-only DB function change, PK-applied; this register pass docs/registers + 1 repo migration-record file, 2026-06-26):** **H3.1** — `public.write_render_log` now computes `attempt_number` itself as **(count of prior `m.post_render_log` rows for the same `(post_draft_id, slide_id)`) + 1**, instead of relying on the column DEFAULT `1`. **Applied to prod (`mbkmaxqhsohbtwsqolns`) manually by PK via `CREATE OR REPLACE` and verified PASS earlier this lane; this register pass = docs/registers + ONE repo migration-record file — 0 app / 0 function / 0 DB apply / 0 deploy / 0 dashboard UI / 0 caller change / 0 pipeline-fixer / 0 backfill.** CE `main == origin/main == 6fb1f8a` (pre-edit). **(1) Live verification (read-only, 2026-06-26):** function body **md5 `baa3531ebe1d3702f6ca8a60f77fdfe8` → `7aa8e8910ff72db396a5cd805f305f8e`**; **single 13-arg overload** (overloads=1); **SECURITY DEFINER retained**; **`search_path=public` retained**; **owner `postgres` retained**; **EXECUTE grants `postgres` + `service_role` only** (PUBLIC/anon/authenticated none) — **all UNCHANGED**. Auto-compute is **live**. **(2) Scope:** FUNCTION-BODY-ONLY; signature unchanged (13 args); no table DDL; no grant change; **no caller/worker change** (image-worker / video-worker / heygen-worker all call the same RPC unaffected). **Telemetry-only** — changes a *logged value*, never a control decision (no path consumes `attempt_number`). **(3) NO backfill** — the **2649 pre-existing rows remain `attempt_number = 1`**; new rows on repeat-render drafts increment going forward. **(4) Grouping key** `(post_draft_id, slide_id)` null-safe (`IS NOT DISTINCT FROM`); null draft → fall back to `1`; `m.post_render_log` schema-qualified in both SELECT and INSERT (search-path-safe). **(5) Gate trail:** `db-rls-auditor` **PASS** (no must-fix; signature identity, grant preservation, SECURITY DEFINER + search_path, schema-qualification, no DDL/RLS change, definer-read sound, **`get_advisors(security)` no NEW finding**) → `ask_chatgpt_review` **WARN-explainable** (verdict `partial`, `review_id 6f877cac-823b-49fe-9e4c-c48fdda7ce48`; sole objection = the concurrency race, classed `policy_decision` not `concrete_defect`) → PK gate (migration apply HARD STOP) → **PK-applied**. **(6) ACCEPTED CONCURRENCY RACE (recorded telemetry-only limitation before H3.2):** `SELECT count(*)` + `INSERT` are not atomic, so concurrent renders of the same `(post_draft_id, slide_id)` can write a duplicate `attempt_number`; no unique constraint rejects it and no control path consumes it → **no functional risk**. Exactness (advisory lock / unique index + retry) is **deferred to H3.2**. **(7) Repo record:** added `supabase/migrations/20260626000000_h3_1_write_render_log_attempt_number_autocompute.sql` (migration name `h3_1_write_render_log_attempt_number_autocompute`; exact applied forward SQL). The change was applied via `CREATE OR REPLACE` (not `apply_migration`) so there is **NO `supabase_migrations` ledger row** — the **repo file is the record** (same backfill-carry pattern as **v3.94** publish_origin / the Lane-3A resolver; the 14-digit prefix is a repo-record stamp, apply-date known / exact time not recorded, ordered after the last ledger migration `20260618092646`). **OPEN CARRY: H3.2 retry cap remains OPEN** (bounded-retry / exactness policy not yet implemented). **DO NOT START (unprompted):** H3.2 / retry-cap implementation · backfill of the legacy `=1` rows · advisory-lock/unique-index exactness · B1-v2 · broad Creative Library production wiring · pipeline-fixer · dashboard work. Authority impact: **none beyond the recorded H3.1 telemetry value** (render content paths, governance, publish, roadmap[`04_phases`], T1 unchanged; AI proposes, PK approves). patterns may reference assets; assets do NOT sit beneath patterns)** → (compose) → Template Families → (instantiated as) → Creative Instances → Evidence. **First-class governed concepts:** Style Guides, Assets, Creative Patterns, Template Families, Creative Instances, Evidence. **Foundation PRESERVED (explicitly unchanged — additive evolution, NOT a rewrite):** governed assets, `resolve_brand_assets()`, resolver scope, provider-ownership model, evidence-first governance, intake framework, review-packet workflow, PK approval gate. **Registry direction (declarative only, NOT consumed by production workers):** next phase extends the declarative registry with `style_guide`, `patterns[]`, `composed_of_patterns[]`, and a generalised evidence model. **Sprint reframe:** Creative Library Expansion **Lane A — Template Factory → Lane A — Creative Design System**; > **✅ v3.69 CREATIVE + RENDER INTELLIGENCE — character-architecture brief LANDED (docs-only; nothing implemented, 2026-06-19):** Architecture for how Creative Intelligence (CI) and Render Intelligence (RI) work around Character Model v0. **0 DB / 0 migration / 0 code / 0 RPC / 0 EF deploy / 0 provider call / 0 marker write / 0 avatar-selection change / 0 AGP activation / 0 CI-or-RI implementation.** **Brief:** `docs/briefs/creative-render-intelligence-character-architecture.md` (companion to `character-model-v0-brand-host-designation.md`). **Definitions:** CI = "what to say + who says it"; RI = "how to physically produce it"; Character Model v0 = the identity CONTRACT between them. **Separation:** CI owns topic / angle / hook / platform-targeting / format-recommendation / narrator_mode / tone / series-structure / brand-host-or-persona **SUGGESTION**; RI owns provider / avatar-vs-non-avatar path / `render_style` / asset-eligibility / cost / latency / quality / platform-capability / fallback. **Boundary (load-bearing):** CI may SUGGEST identity/persona; RI RESOLVES identity → eligible asset/provider; **CI must NOT directly pick avatar assets; RI must NOT pick topic/angle/hook.** **Realistic vs animated** = asset-level `render_style` / RI decision — style variants of the SAME host identity, NOT a separate character, NOT a CI decision; active hosts realistic, animated dormant/unproven (do NOT activate animated; do NOT conflate render_style with the avatar-vs-non-avatar path). **Instrument LATER (record-only):** CI attribution completeness (host identity, narrator_mode, platform, format, tone, possibly hook/angle/topic if already available) + Render-path telemetry (provider, render_style, cost, latency, success/failure, fallback_taken, quality/outcome). **DO NOT automate yet:** no Creative performance panel; no live avatar/persona/style-driven selection; no provider auto-switching; no animated-variant activation; no Branch B; no AGP activation; **no performance optimisation until a real engagement signal exists.** **Recommended future slices (DO NOT IMPLEMENT YET):** CI slice = Creative attribution completeness (record-only); > **✅ v3.63 F-INSIGHTS-WORKER-WINDOW30-90-FRESHNESS — insights-worker v14.4.0 RECOVERY DEPLOYED + VERIFIED (windows 30/90 unfrozen; code-only EF change, 2026-06-19):** The stale worker-owned `m.post_format_performance` windows 30/90 are **recovered and live-verified fresh.** **Root cause (proven, read-only):** the insights-worker EF was killed by the ~150s wall-clock limit on every run (HTTP 504/546 at ~150.5s) — its handler swept **ALL 4 FB clients sequentially** while **ignoring the per-client cron body selector** the 4 crons already send (`{"client_publish_profile_id":"<uuid>"}`, jobid 87-90, staggered 03:00/05/10/15), so the tail `computeFormatPerformance` (sole writer of windows 30/90 since Fix-2 narrowed `refresh_post_format_performance` to `{7,0}`) never committed → windows frozen since 2026-06-12/06-13. Collection looked fresh because per-post `m.post_performance` upserts land incrementally (masking the freeze); cron `job_run_details` read "succeeded/1 row" only because `net.http_post` is fire-and-forget (records the enqueue, not the EF's 504). **Fix (insights-worker v14.2.0 → v14.4.0, single file `supabase/functions/insights-worker/index.ts`):** (#1) **aggregation-first** — `computeFormatPerformance(all active client_ids)` runs FIRST, global, before collection, so the cheap window write can never be starved (a wall-clock kill is uncatchable; running the tail first is the durable freshness guarantee); (#2) **honor the existing cron selector** — parse the body defensively and scope collection to ONE client/run; **D-A2 safe default** — missing/invalid body → aggregation-only, collect nothing (`no_client_scope`), never the full sweep; additive `scope_mode` response field. Collection/metric/engagement/token/`raw_payload` logic **byte-identical**. **Deploy facts:** commit **`e0fc5e4`** merged + pushed to `main` (origin **0/0**); deployed **insights-worker function version 67** via `--no-verify-jwt` (PK-run); **`verify_jwt=false` preserved** (authoritative `get_edge_function` + header-less GET 200). **Gates:** ef-builder (isolated worktree, `deno check` exit 0) → branch-warden **safe** → external **design** review `6754590e` (escalated → PK resolved; decisions **D-A2** + keep global aggregation) → external **final-diff** review `53724307` (**agree**/proceed) → PK deploy authorization → merge+push (orchestrator) → PK-run deploy. **Live verification (read-only):** GET → `insights-worker-v14.4.0`; bodyless POST → `scope_mode=no_client_scope`, processed 0, **`windows_computed=50`**, 3.8s; client-scoped POST (Invegent) → `scope_mode=client_scoped`, **36/36** collected, 200; DB confirms **windows 30 & 90 `computed_at` ≈ 2026-06-19 04:42 UTC (50 distinct per-row worker timestamps)**, replacing the frozen 06-13/06-12; windows 0/7 unaffected (cron-owned 03:15). **Residual (mitigated, NOT freshness-blocking):** at the observed ~3s/post, the two large clients **NDIS-Yarns (253 eligible)** and **Property-Pulse (240)** cap at `MAX_POSTS_PER_CLIENT=50` so their *collection* phase runs ~150s and may still 504 — but **aggregation-first commits 30/90 in ~3.8s before any collection**, so windows stay fresh regardless, and per-post upserts make incremental progress. **Carry change: F-INSIGHTS-WORKER-WINDOW30-90-FRESHNESS → CLOSED (recovered + verified).** **OPENED this pass: `F-INSIGHTS-WORKER-COLLECTION-RUNTIME` (P3/P4)** — bring large-client collection fully under budget (lower `MAX_POSTS_PER_CLIENT` to ~25-30 and/or parallelize per-post Graph fetches); separate code lane, not freshness-blocking. **Other carries unchanged.** **Register commit pending PK instruction — this pass PREPARES the reconciliation; no register commit/push yet.** Brief `docs/briefs/f-insights-worker-window30-90-freshness.md`; result `docs/briefs/results/f-insights-worker-window30-90-freshness.md`. > **✅ v3.61 INSIGHTS FIX 2 — F-INSIGHTS-FIX2-AGGREGATION-OWNERSHIP CLOSED AS STALE / ALREADY-IMPLEMENTED (read-only readiness review + register reconciliation, docs-only, 2026-06-18):** The Insights Fix 2 aggregation-ownership decision (Option B, PK 2026-06-13) is **already satisfied in production** — **this pass touches `00_sync_state.md` + `00_action_list.md` only: 0 DB / 0 code / 0 migration / 0 deploy / 0 Advisor behaviour change / 0 production mutation.** **Problem (recap):** the 03:15 cron `public.refresh_post_format_performance()` and the insights-worker `computeFormatPerformance` both wrote `m.post_format_performance` window-30 on unique key `(client_id, ice_format_key, rolling_window_days)` → dual-writer clobber; the aggregation-ownership ambiguity made whichever ran later overwrite the other. **Option B (PK 2026-06-13):** scope the cron windows `{7, 30, 0}` → `{7, 0}` so the worker becomes sole owner of window-30. **Current-state evidence (read-only this lane):** live `public.refresh_post_format_performance()` is **SECURITY DEFINER, `search_path = pg_catalog, public, m`**, and its windows CTE reads **`unnest(ARRAY[7, 0])`** — **`30` appears nowhere in the body** (`mentions_30 = false`); the cron **no longer writes rolling window 30**. The insights-worker (`supabase/functions/insights-worker/index.ts:319`) loops **`for (const windowDays of [30, 90])`** → **worker remains sole owner of windows 30 and 90.** **Ownership is now DISJOINT** — cron {7, 0} ∩ worker {30, 90} = ∅ → **the 03:15 dual-writer clobber is structurally eliminated.** This is exactly Option B's prescribed end-state. **Row evidence (`m.post_format_performance`, 4 clients):** window-0 + window-7 fresh through **2026-06-18 03:15** (cron-stamped); window-30 last written **2026-06-13 03:15**; window-90 last written **2026-06-12 03:16**. **Verdict: the original Insights Fix 2 apply packet is STALE / a no-op → RETIRED. > **✅ v3.45 SERIES v2 STAGE 3.5a — PLATFORM-AWARE OUTLINE GENERATION DEPLOYED & VERIFIED (series-outline v1.3.0; register reconciliation, docs-only, 2026-06-14):** The series outline generator is now **capability-aware**. Previously it received only `series.platform` (singular) and hard-clamped `recommended_format` to `text|image_quote|carousel` in BOTH the prompt and the validation whitelist — so a YouTube-targeted series was **structurally incapable of emitting a video format** and every YouTube child was rejected downstream (zero YouTube output). **Shipped (series-outline EF ONLY — single file `supabase/functions/series-outline/index.ts`, commit `65d6dc4372338c2b9862097eec87cc2c8945d728`):** (a) reads `series.platforms[]` with fallback to `[series.platform]`; (b) calls `public.get_studio_capabilities(client_id)` — the SAME resolver Single Post / Studio uses; (c) computes the VALID format set = formats whose state ∈ {enabled, enabled_unproven} on EVERY selected eligible platform (**intersection**, so the single per-episode format is publishable on all targets) + `video_only` detection; (d) feeds that set into the prompt AND uses it as the validation whitelist (resolver-driven, **not** the old hardcoded `text|image_quote|carousel`); (e) if NO format is valid across the selected set, **FAILS LOUD `no_valid_format_for_platform_set` (HTTP 422)** — never silently picks text; capability resolution runs BEFORE the `outline_pending` move so a failure leaves the series unchanged. **Interim behaviour (intentional, recorded):** mixed **FB+IG+LI+YT currently resolves to `video_short_avatar` only** (the cross-platform intersection under current taxonomy) — **intentional interim for safety**; true per-platform-per-episode format diversity remains **DEFERRED**. **Deployed facts:** live version **series-outline-v1.3.0**; deployed via Supabase CLI **`--no-verify-jwt`** (`verify_jwt=false` preserved); pre-deploy `deno check` exit 0; D-01 **`b45da2c8-9189-491f-ad83-e9bc90936e8b`** (proceed / agree / medium risk / high confidence / escalate=false). **Post-deploy read-only V-checks (no production series mutated):** GET → `series-outline-v1.3.0`; POST with missing/invalid `x-series-key` → 401; header-less GET → 200 (verify_jwt false, not regressed); resolver dry-check (read-only `get_studio_capabilities`, function NOT invoked) — YouTube-only → all-video set, Instagram excludes text, FB+IG+LI+YT intersection = `["video_short_avatar"]`, empty intersection → 422 (code-verified); 0 `c.content_series` rows mutated during verification. **DOWNSTREAM GATES UNCHANGED:** `fan_out_episode`, `create_manual_slot_internal`, the per-platform capability rejection, Advisor, compliance, render, publisher all untouched — the whitelist + the downstream gate remain hard backstops. **Stage 3.5a = COMPLETE / DEPLOYED / VERIFIED; Stage 3.5b (retry_episode platform-awareness) = OPEN next carry (NOT started).** **Carries (NEW / carried-forward — NOT done):** **F-SERIES-RETRY-PLATFORM-AWARENESS** (P2 — Stage 3.5b: make `retry_episode` capability/platform-aware, mirroring 3.5a); **per-platform-per-episode format diversity** (P3 — replace the interim single-intersection format with per-platform-native episode formats); **F-SLOT-SCHEDULE-FIDELITY** (P3 — schedule fidelity lane, pre-existing); **persona capture lane** (P3 — episode persona_label/avatar_preference/persona_notes capture surface). **Lane footprint: 1 EF deploy (series-outline v1.3.0); this register pass is docs-only — 0 code / 0 DB / 0 migration / 0 schema / 0 UI / 0 publisher / 0 retry_episode / 0 fan_out_episode / 0 production mutation.** Authority impact: none (outline is upstream content planning; as-built decision flow + T1 unchanged). Series v2 Stage 1/2/3 + publisher v1.9.0 guard, cc-0015 / cc-0020 / OBS-0A / PRV / IG / YT lanes preserved unchanged.

> **✅ v3.44 FACEBOOK PUBLISHER ASSETLESS-RELEASE GUARD — CLOSED & DEPLOYED (publisher v1.9.0; register reconciliation, docs-only, 2026-06-14):** The Facebook asset-less publish leak is **RESOLVED for Facebook**. Live incident — FB post `962399936961457_122114734587268380`, draft `1d34577bbb5a`, format `image_quote`, `image_status='failed'`, `image_url` absent — published as a silent **text feed post** because the old image hold gate only caught `image_status='pending'` (a `failed` asset fell through → `hasImage=false` → `/feed`); video formats had no asset gate at all. **Shipped fix (Facebook `publisher` edge function ONLY):** new dependency-free guard `supabase/functions/publisher/guard.ts` (`classifyFbFormat` + pure `decideAssetGuard`); updated `supabase/functions/publisher/index.ts`; validation harness `docs/briefs/publisher-assetless-guard-validation.test.ts`. **Shipped safety behaviour:** (a) **image-required formats no longer fall back to text** — `image_quote` requires `image_status='generated'` + `image_url`, else BLOCK `image_required_but_<status>`; (b) **carousel-required formats no longer downgrade silently** — require generated + ≥2 slides, else BLOCK `carousel_incomplete_slides:N`; (c) **video/animated formats no longer publish as text on FB**; (d) **unsupported FB video is blocked with `fb_video_publish_not_supported_interim`** (the FB publisher has no video publish path); (e) **failed/missing/pending-timeout assets are skipped/blocked with an `asset_guard_blocked:<reason>` reason** (queue `status='skipped'`, terminal/not-re-locked, + an audit `post_publish status='failed'` row), **draft preserved**; pending remains a retryable hold (the assetless-publish-on-timeout behaviour was removed); **text still publishes via feed** (unchanged). **This is an INTERIM guard / "T2-Lite" (existence/status only) — NOT full T2** (no OCR / transcript / visual / brand / audio QA). **Deployed facts:** merge commit `0216b79`; close-out commit `7a4e3c3`; runtime close-out `docs/runtime/sessions/2026-06-14-publisher-assetless-guard-closeout.md`; live version **publisher-v1.9.0** (Supabase function version **91**); **`verify_jwt=false` confirmed authoritatively** (deployed via Supabase CLI `--no-verify-jwt`, per the verify_jwt deploy gotcha); D-01 **`fcf2b32d-f234-4a36-bb82-60cfe8038e82`** (verdict agree / medium / high / proceed). Pre-deploy validation: `deno check` exit 0 + `deno test` **21/21 PASS** against the real guard functions; post-deploy read-only V-checks: version v1.9.0, verify_jwt false, **0 asset-required FB posts published as text since deploy**, current FB queue (2 `image_quote` generated + 1 `carousel` generated) **not stranded**. **Carries (NEW, carried-forward — NOT done):** **F-PUBLISHER-ASSETGUARD-LI-IG-YT** (P2 — equivalent interim assetless guard audit/patch for the LinkedIn, Instagram and YouTube publishers; same leak class, not yet guarded); **full T2 remains the durable replacement** for this interim existence/status guard (DEFERRED); **FB video publishing support remains separate feature work** (video formats currently blocked on FB by design). **Rollback (preserved):** redeploy prior **publisher-v1.8.0** (git blob `56b1d1da`) via Supabase CLI **with `--no-verify-jwt`**; **no DB rollback required** (guard writes only existing columns/values). **Lane footprint: 1 EF deploy (publisher v1.9.0); this register pass is docs-only — 0 code / 0 DB / 0 migration / 0 schema / 0 dashboard / 0 other-publisher / 0 FB-video-publishing / 0 production mutation.** Authority impact: none (publisher is downstream of the decision tree; as-built flow + T1 unchanged). > **🔴 v3.42 F-OPTIONC-ENGAGEMENT-EVIDENCE-NULL DIAGNOSED — engagement evidence feed structurally broken; carry opened P2; Option C stays PARKED (read-only investigation + register-only close, 2026-06-12):** `m.post_format_performance.avg_engagement_rate` is effectively NULL despite healthy post_count because of three stacked defects. **D1 (primary):** insights-worker v14.1.0 computes `engagement_rate = engaged_users/reach` but `engaged_users` is never obtained — the `post_engaged_users` Graph metric fails **526/526 FB rows** across all four clients (raw_payload.failed_metrics; systematic; introduced v14.0.0) and the reactions+comments+shares fallback is **0 on 526/526** (failed field reads coerced to 0, indistinguishable from genuine zero) → engagement_rate NULL on every FB row even though reach>0 on 322/526 and FB collection is otherwise fresh (06-12) and cron-scheduled (ny 03:00 / cfw 03:05 / pp 03:10 / invegent 03:15 + insights-feedback-daily 03:30 — FB schedule layer healthy). **D2:** dual-writer clobber on `m.post_format_performance` — insights-worker's `computeFormatPerformance` (per-client ~03:01–03:16, windows 30+90, all-platform, captures YT engagement) vs `refresh_post_format_performance()` cron 03:15 (windows 7/30/0, FB-only via `reach IS NOT NULL`) on the same PK; the refresh **clobbers worker-produced window-30 values with NULL FB-only averages — exactly the window the Advisor reads**. Survivor proof: all non-NULL avg rows are window-90 or YT-only-video combos stamped 03:01/03:12. **D3:** YouTube structurally excluded — YT perf rows carry engagement on 20/62 but **reach NULL 62/62** so the refresh filter drops all; YT insights stale 05-29 / manual-only (existing carry). **LinkedIn + Instagram have zero insight rows.** **Advisor impact:** ai-worker coerces NULL→0, injecting a fabricated "0.0% avg engagement (N posts)" summary per job — misleading, not merely absent. **Recommended fix sequence (recorded, NOT approved/implemented; each gated):** (1) FB engagement repair in insights-worker incl. raw-failure visibility (ef_deploy); (2) aggregation ownership — stop the 03:15 clobber (cheapest: retire redundant refresh cron, worker owns table, keep window-7); (3) YT reach/views mapping + YT cron; (4) Advisor bad-evidence shielding (don't render NULL as 0.0%). **Option C cannot become evidence-based until the feed is repaired** — Monday gate posture confirmed. **if that predicate is ever weakened the Public default becomes unsafe and must be re-reviewed.** **No backfill (proven):** the only YouTube write is the multipart `videos.insert` in `uploadToYouTube` (no `videos.update`/privacy-patch path); already-published drafts (`youtube_video_id` set / `video_status` not `generated`) fail the SELECT + pre-upload reconcile guard, so they are never re-selected and never re-uploaded — PK's manual Public history is untouched. **Non-YouTube publishers unaffected (proven):** repo-wide grep for `privacyStatus`/`privacy_status`/`unlisted` matches ONLY `youtube-publisher/index.ts`; the other five publishers (`wordpress-`/`linkedin-`/`linkedin-zapier-`/`instagram-`/generic `publisher`) have no such field, and deploying `youtube-publisher` redeploys no other function. **Deploy (PK-approved `ef_deploy` only):** `supabase functions deploy youtube-publisher --no-verify-jwt --project-ref mbkmaxqhsohbtwsqolns` — SUCCESS (Docker-not-running warning benign; ### 2026-05-24 Sydney — v3.05: YouTube OAuth Production restore (root cause found + both channels publishing)

**Outcome:** YouTube publishing **RESTORED**. The prior (1 May) audit was stale; PK was right it had been fixed in early May then re-broke. **Root cause definitively identified: the Google OAuth app was in "Testing" publishing status, which caps refresh tokens at 7 days.** PK moved the app to Production + re-exchanged tokens; two single-draft live tests published successfully, proving both channels' tokens now refresh. Backlog released (fresh) + soft-retired (stale). Separately: cc-0019 brief authored + reviewed clean (brief only), and a read-only slotting AI-cost-waste audit.

**Root-cause evidence (read-only):**
| Fact | Value |
|---|---|
| Last successful publish | PP 12 May 07:45 UTC (11 total); NY 11 May 09:45 UTC (2 total) |
| Re-break | Day after each last success; `invalid_grant: Token expired or revoked` |
| Token lifetime post-5 May reconnect | **NY 7.00 days, PP 7.92 days** → Testing-mode 7-day cap fingerprint |
| Stored token | Genuine `1//` refresh token (103 chars) in `c.client_channel.config`; no expiry field stored |
| Dashboard "Expires 2031" | Cosmetic — callback hardcodes `now()+5y` ("tokens don't expire"); publisher never reads it |
| OAuth flow | `auth/route.ts` correctly sets `access_type=offline`+`prompt=consent`; `callback/route.ts` stores token + fake expiry |

**Fix + verification (governed):**
| Step | Detail |
|---|---|
| Fix | PK moved OAuth app Testing→Production + re-exchanged (NY token_updated_at 10:48:22, PP 10:49:05 UTC) |
| PP test | mig `yt_token_verify_reset_one_pp_draft_20260524` (draft `2afce74e…`) → invoke req 126325 → **`ma6EG1fz4XQ`** published 10:57:23 UTC |
| NY test | mig `yt_token_verify_reset_one_ny_draft_20260524` (draft `b9860637…`) → invoke req 126339 → **`qp-ZGm8lNIo`** published 11:02:24 UTC |
| Backlog | mig `yt_backlog_release_fresh_softretire_stale_20260524`: release ≥12 May (NY 6 + PP 7 = 13 → generated, draining); retire <12 May (NY 3 + PP 11 = 14 → archived_stale) |
| Untouched | failed-out-of-guard NY 3 + PP 9 (non-uploadable format / non-approved); CFW + Invegent (never connected) |
| D-01 | sql_destructive `82443c8c` (PP+NY tests), `5f7bfc52` (batch) — both partial/type-c, escalated, PK pre-approved |

**Publisher reliability gap (F-YT-FAILED-NO-RETRY):** youtube-publisher v1.6.0 selects only `video_status='generated'`+`approval_status='approved'`; its catch handler sets failures to terminal `video_status='failed'`, which it never re-selects. A token outage therefore silently freezes the entire rendered backlog. Candidate brief: retryable vs terminal failure, or a retry sweep. *(v3.06: brief authored — `docs/briefs/yt-publisher-failed-no-retry.md`, `bee872aa`; Unit-B patched to live 3-bucket recovery `a3f329f3`; plan_review CLEAN `abf6f63c`→`f89c23cf`; execution gated.)*

**cc-0019 brief (publish-eligibility gate, brief only):** `docs/briefs/cc-0019-publish-eligibility-gate.md` — `81cb414` (create) → `01a6cdf` (harden §4 transition handling). Design: `m.is_publish_eligible(client_id, platform)` + fill-gate in `fill_pending_slots` + ai-worker preflight, to stop AI token spend on drafts with no live publish path (measured ~12% waste on disabled NY/PP IG). plan_review `a75c78f6` (partial/type-c) → re-fire `ff05c65e` (agree/clean). **NOT implemented** — execution gated on sql_destructive (Unit A migration) + ef_deploy (Unit B ai-worker) + PK approval. *(v3.06 CORRECTION: Unit A is in fact IMPLEMENTED — migration `20260524091020` applied 24 May; Unit B (ai-worker preflight) NOT implemented per deployed ai-worker v2.12.0. This "brief only" line was stale.)*

**Slotting audit bonus finding:** `m.materialise_slots` references `publish_enabled` only inside the per-platform format-preference lookup — a disabled profile yields NULL format → slot still inserted (defaults `image_quote`). Disablement was wired to format-selection, not skip. Two switches never unified: `client_publish_profile.publish_enabled` (publish) vs `client_publish_schedule.enabled` (materialise). cc-0019 is the unification.

**Hard stops respected v3.05:**
- cc-0019 brief only — 0 gate migration, 0 EF deploy, `fill_pending_slots` unchanged, `is_publish_eligible` not created
- YT mutations: exactly 3 guarded migrations (draft `video_status` only) + 2 publisher invokes. 0 cron change / 0 EF deploy / 0 client enablement change / 0 queue/profile mutation / 0 hard delete

Flagged, not folded in (unverified SHAs in-context; detail in transcript `2026-05-24-07-57-08-ice-ig-restore-fresh-restart-cost-gate.txt`). *(v3.06: substantially discharged — publisher `bc78511e` + 7 migration files `8738c3a0`; residual operational only.)*

## 📜 G1 convention (the rule)

Unchanged. **v3.05 recorded via the surgical discipline: new session file `f9ddd51` created; sync_state + action_list patched with read-HEAD-first `create_or_update_file` calls passing the just-read blob SHAs (sync_state `7d2b0eb8`, action_list `ecaf50f8`) to detect concurrent edits.** **v3.06 recorded the same way: session file `1219aff0` created; sync_state + action_list patched read-HEAD-first with blob SHAs passed (action_list `23972a0a`, sync_state `d8f18cbd`). Post-close, the two `00_` files received a further narrow surgical patch recording the F-YT-FAILED-NO-RETRY plan_review CLEAN outcome (`abf6f63c`→`f89c23cf`) + Unit-B brief patch (`a3f329f3`) + the +2 plan_review D-01 tally — same read-HEAD-first sha-passed discipline.** **v3.07 (doc-patch housekeeping): NO per-session file created and Dashboard PHASES leg N/A — PK explicitly scoped the close to the two `00_` files (doc-only session, no phase change). sync_state + action_list patched read-HEAD-first with blob SHAs passed (sync_state `df1f44ac`; action_list re-read for its own write). This is a deliberate, PK-scoped deviation from the full G1 4-way; a per-session file can be added later if the full ritual is wanted.** **v3.08 (Avatar→YouTube milestone): repo reconciliation of an already-live pipeline; recorded into the two `00_` files read-HEAD-first with blob SHAs passed (sync_state `29dffe9d`; action_list `ba02a6ff`). No per-session file + Dashboard PHASES leg N/A (PK-scoped to the two `00_` files; no new deploy, no phase change). The EF source + continuity docs were reconciled to `main` in commits `521b053b`+`194e0792` (EFs) and `04294d23` (docs) ahead of this `00_` rebuild. Post-milestone narrow patch (2026-05-26): cc-0019 Unit B re-verification recorded — re-read HEAD sha-passed (sync_state `cea33088`); discharged the "re-verify against v2.13.0" carry by confirming Unit B still absent in ai-worker v2.13.0 (`8204a5c7`).** Dashboard roadmap/PHASES leg N/A this cycle (operational / doc-only, no phase change). `decisions.md` not touched.

**Lesson surfaced (v3.05):** an audit committed to memory/docs goes stale — when YT was reported "fixed then broke again," the right move was to re-run the audit against live data rather than trust the 1 May finding. And recording only the *symptom*-level fix (reconnect token) let the same root cause (Testing-mode 7-day expiry) recur silently ≥3 times. Record causes, not just fixes (L-v3.05-a).

**Lesson surfaced (v3.06):** deployed state and the repo can silently diverge — the deployed IG publisher was 4 versions ahead of repo `main`, so a routine redeploy would have reverted the live fix; and chat-applied migrations (`apply_migration`) write the DB but never commit a file, leaving the repo's migration history stale. Verify deployed-vs-repo before redeploying, and backfill chat-applied migrations same-session (L-v3.06-a). Also: when a doc asserts something is "not implemented," verify against the live DB/EF before propagating it — cc-0019 Unit A had in fact been applied. And the F-YT plan_review re-confirmed L62: a partial/type-c verdict that echoes self-disclosed weak evidence is resolved by satisfying it against live data (here: confirming `video_status`=text/no-CHECK + bucketing the 30 failed drafts, then patching Unit B), then re-firing — which returned clean.

**Lesson surfaced (v3.07):** the action_list "doc patch" carries were one-line *intentions*, not specified diffs — only cc-0017c had a documented v-next scope (in its v2.85 apply session), so only it could be patched faithfully; the rest had to be deferred rather than blind-patched. Separately, the GitHub bridge offers no str_replace, so editing any large doc means re-emitting the whole file — an L41 clobber/drift risk that makes large-brief patches (cc-0017a 72KB, cc-0010A 107KB, etc.) genuinely safer as CC surgical edits than chat full-file rewrites (L-v3.07-a). And "promote a lesson" could not be executed because the canonical L37–L65 definition home + numbering convention are not recorded anywhere locatable — promotion by assumption was correctly declined.

**Lesson reinforced (v3.08):** the Avatar→YouTube reconciliation re-exercised the bridge-native squash discipline — SHA-equality between the pushed blob and the source branch blob is the definitive byte-parity proof for a copy-style reconciliation, and a self-caught mis-scoped `files` array (commit 1 shipped 1 of 3 EFs) was flagged openly and corrected rather than passed silently. L41 reinforced again (the two `00_` writes done read-HEAD-first, sha-passed). L-v2.85-e reinforced (the 12-file reconciliation was split into EF / continuity-doc / `00_` commits to keep each push within budget). Post-milestone, cc-0019 Unit B was re-verified against the now-live ai-worker v2.13.0 (`8204a5c7`) — confirmed STILL absent (the avatar A2/A3 changes are orthogonal to the eligibility preflight), discharging the "re-verify against v2.13.0" carry without any EF edit (absence is expected, not a missing implementation, since Unit A's fill-gate already covers the primary waste vector).
